# 《中国植物志》植物中文正式名的订正

<p><span style="font-size: 14px;">（井井只是改了改格式2333）<br  /></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">原文名为《&lt;中国植物志&gt;植物中文普通名的订正和读音的统一》，知网链接已于文末给出。</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">文章发布前已获得作者刘夙老师的授权。</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">全文目录如下：</span><br  /></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">一、改重名</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">二、和种下等级有关的中文名订正</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1. 种和自动名中文名不匹配的订正：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2.由种下等级旧命名法所得中文名的订正：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">三、正字</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1.改掉少数民族的旧称：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2.改掉部分 GBK 字库中未收录的冷僻字：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 3.异体字的订正：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 4.别字的订正：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">四、读音的统一</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1.多音字的整理：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2.单音字的准确定音：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 3.科属中文名的普通话白读：</span></p><p><span style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);font-size: 14px;">附：科属中文名中的同音名称&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);"></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;"></span><br  /></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">井井注：</span><span style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);"></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">①为更好地区分文中内容，编者已将</span><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(0, 128, 255);">中文正式名用蓝色标出</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">，</span><span style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;color: rgb(71, 193, 168);">学名用绿色标出</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">，<span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(255, 104, 39);">有争议之处及各种观点用黄色标出</span>。<br  /></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">②本文篇幅较长，无法一次全部推出，故分（上）、（下）两篇。本篇为上篇，取目录前三章内容，</span><span style="font-size: 14px;text-decoration: underline;">因此本文标题也与原文标题不同</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">。<br  /></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">③原文中有一些小bug，本文以改正，在此不一一指出。<br  /></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">④封面选自</span><span style="font-size: 14px;text-decoration: underline;">《康熙字典·申集上》</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">。<br  /></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">⑤<span style="font-size: 14px;">本文编者对某些字的读音尚存疑，但在此遵从原文</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">，不予修改。</span><br  /></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">⑥<span style="font-size: 14px;">为最大程度上避免学名造成的排版问题，本文字体可能较小，还请见谅。</span></span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;">正文如下：</span></p><p><span style="font-size: 14px;"><br  /></span></p><h1 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;"><span style="font-family:宋体;">引</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span style="font-family:宋体;">言</span></h1><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">共</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">80</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">126</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">册的《中国植物志》（以下简称《植物志》），历时</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">35</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">年，终于在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2004</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">年</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">10</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">月全部出版完成。它是迄今为止是目前世界上篇幅最大的植物志，也是关于中国维管束植物的最为完整的志书。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">《植物志》给中国的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">万多种维管束植物都赋予了中文名，这对于中国的科技术语研究来说，也是一个很了不起的成就。《植物志》所收载植物的中文正名（区别于中文别名，以下简称“别名”）可以看成是目前最好的植物中文名称的规范，迄今还没有另一套植物中文名系统的合理性能够超过《植物志》的系统。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不过，也应指出，由于编纂时间较长，参与人员较多，《植物志》中的植物中文名正名还存在少数问题，可以分为三类</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:windowtext;">：</span></p><p style="margin-left:14px;text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">个别类群重名；</span></p><p style="margin-left:14px;text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">种下等级命名法不统一；</span></p><p style="margin-left:14px;text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">部分名称有不符合现代汉语规范的异体字和别字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为了方便科研人员和社会各届人士使用《植物志》，为了方便《植物志》的数字化，特别是为了促进植物中文名的规范化、使之符合现代汉语的规范，有必要对这些问题进行订正。同时，基于同样的要求，《植物志》中的植物中文名正名的读音也有必要统一，建立规范。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">笔者一直对《植物志》植物中文正名的整理工作抱有兴趣。在帮助中国科学院植物所网络中心建设数据库的过程中，有幸得以利用他们录入的《植物志》植物名录数据库，对这项工作进行初步尝试。本文就是这些初步工作的总结。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">有一点需要说明的是，植物中文正名的拟名权，最终应归于各个类群的分类学研究者，这是植物分类学界普遍赞同的做法；同时，保持植物中文正名的稳定性，也是植物中文名拟定的最高原则之一。因此，笔者在下文中所做的植物中文正名的订正，属于一种“消极性”订正，即仅在某一名称存在上述三类问题中的某一类或某几类、非订正不可时，才进行订正，否则就不做任何更动，即使这一名称在别的方面仍存在不妥之处。例如，茄科植物</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Solanum tuberosum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的最通用的中文名是“马铃薯”，但《植物志》茄科作者基于其他考虑，选用了“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阳芋</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”作为这一植物的中文正名，虽然笔者觉得不尽合理，但“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阳芋</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这一名称本身并不存在重名、异体字或别字的问题，所以笔者未做任何订正。又如一位网友向笔者指出，中药“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">防己</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的“己”字本作“巳”，巳在此指蛇，“防巳”是指该药可以做蛇药，写成“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">防己</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”则不通；但笔者基于上述原因，也未对这一名称做修改。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">以下如不另加说明，凡称“植物中文名”，均指《植物志》的植物中文正名。由于科、属、种是国际植物命名法规（以下简称</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">ICBN</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）规定的分类群的主要等级，同时也限于笔者精力，下文仅对《植物志》中科、属、种（含种下等级）的中文正名做了订正和读音的统一，而暂未涉及其他等级如族、组、系等的中文正名。</span></p><p style="text-align:left;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span></p><h1 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;"><span style="font-family:宋体;">一、改重名</span></h1><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">分类的内在要求之一，是使各个类群名称不相重复，即一个名称只能对应一个类群（但反过来则不一定成立，一个类群也可能对应多个名称），以使类群名称能够真正成为类群的标识，不致引起混乱。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">ICBN </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">制订了十分严格的规则，以保证类群的学名不相重复，但中文名作为类群的“俗名”，因为没有类似的严格规则的限制，其中一名多物的现象是很普遍的。若要避免引起混乱，便于应用，就必须对“一名多物”进行彻底的整理清除。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">因为在编纂时特别注意到了这点，《植物志》中的重名现象是很少的，即使是种和原种下等级，虽然基本名称相同，但后者仍要通过括注“原亚种”“原变种”等字样和前者区别（虽然有个别科属在编纂时未遵循这一命名格式）。经过整理，《植物志》中有重名</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">69</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">对，其中</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">对为属名相重，即</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">扁穗草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Blysmus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Brylkinia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">钩毛草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Pseudechinolaena</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Kelloggia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">球菊属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Epaltes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bolocephalus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虾子草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Mimulicalyx</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Nechamandra</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其余为种名（含种下等级名）相重。因为在上述</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">对相重的属名中，有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">对也导致了相应的种名相重（如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">扁穗草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的重名导致了</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Blysmuscompressus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Brylkinia caudata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">也重名，均叫“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">扁穗草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”），所以真正的重名只有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">66</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">对。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">马其云在其编著的《中国蕨类植物与种子植物名称总汇》（以下简称《总汇》）一书的“前言与使用说明”中，对重名类群的处理提出了三个原则：</span></p><p style="text-indent:48px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">与科属名称相关的名称优先保留；</span></p><p style="text-indent:48px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">应用广泛或重要书刊上的名称优先保留；</span></p><p style="text-indent:48px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">名称应用时间长的优先保留。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">对于不保留原名的类群的改名，马其云也提出三个原则：</span></p><p style="text-indent:48px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">从原有异名中选一个尚未被其他植物应用的名称为正名；</span></p><p style="text-indent:48px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">新拟名称，以属名为基础，冠以种加词、植物形态特征加词或出产地名加词等组成新名称；</span></p><p style="text-indent:48px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">种类较多的大属，种下分类群若改名，需在原种名前加上述有关各类加词，构成新名称。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">按照上述原则，马其云在该书的正文中对一部分重名做了订正（但遗憾的是，另一部分则仍未订正）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">笔者基本同意马其云总结的上述原则，但认为对其中某些原则不能过分拘泥，要根据具体情况具体分析、灵活解决。下面就对《植物志》</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">66</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">对重名的问题，进行逐一探讨（按原名的音序排列）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">白藤：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Calamus tetradactylus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">棕榈科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）与</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Poranadecora</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">旋花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。马其云已指出，对后者来说，“白藤”只是云南的地方土名，而《中国高等植物图鉴》（以下简称《图鉴》）已将此名用于前者。此外，尽管《植物志》在前者名下列了别名“鸡藤”（后者未列别名），但前者的分布远较后者为广，而且有经济价值（可供编织藤器），且《植物志》棕榈科一卷出版年代较旋花科一卷早，故笔者同意马其云为后者新拟中文名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">白飞蛾藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">扁果薹草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Carex urelytra</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C.caucasica </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">jisaburo-ohwiana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者为种下等级，且《植物志》已列出别名“大井扁果薹”（出自《台湾植物志》），故前者保留原名，后者按大陆的习惯改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大井扁果薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”（同属另有一个种下等级异型菱果薹</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. grallatoria </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> heteroclita</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，也是台湾名，宜按大陆的习惯改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">异型菱果薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">扁穗草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Blysmus compressus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Brylkinia caudata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名，同时</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Blysmus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Brylkinia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">二属也重名。该莎草科植物的分布较禾本科植物为广，且《植物志》莎草科一卷编成较早，故前者保留原名，后者新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">扁穗茅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，属名拟为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">扁穗茅属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，因其在《植物志》系统中前后的几个属多有“茅”字（如羊茅属、鼠茅属、鸭茅属、碱茅属等），而该属植物（仅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">种）也具长芒，符合“茅”字的涵义。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">扁桃：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Amygdalus communis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Mangifera persiciformis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">漆树科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者是重要经济植物，种仁为重要干果，而“扁桃”做为前者的中文名，已经广泛使用，且用以命名了其所属的组</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Amygdalus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Sect. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Amygdalus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。后者虽然也有一定的经济价值（果可食，为良好的庭园和行道绿化树种），但知名度远不如前者。故前者保留原名，后者从《植物志》所列三个别名中，选择“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">天桃木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”作为新的正名（另两个“唛咖”和“酸果”，一为壮语，另一名称涵义太宽泛，均不如天桃木合适）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">长苞灯心草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Juncus leucomelas</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">J.brachyspathus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">灯心草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者在《植物志》中仅为一存疑种，且其种加词意为“短苞”而非长苞，故将后者改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">短苞灯心草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">长柄线蕨：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Colysis elliptica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> longipes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. pedunculata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">水龙骨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者虽为种下等级，但其原变种中文名即为“线蕨”，且“长柄”正是其变种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> longipes </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的直译，而</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pedunculata </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的直译是“具柄的”，没有“长”的含义，故前者保留原名。但马其云将后者中文名改为“长梗线蕨”，并不合适。从字义上讲，“柄”和“梗”并没有区别，因此不如拟为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">具柄线蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，取其种加词直译即可。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">长梗薹草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Carex glossostigma</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C.fulvo-rubescens</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">longistipes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者为种下等级，故改名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">长梗扁果薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">长果驼蹄瓣：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Zygophyllum fabago</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> subsp. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">dolichocarpum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Z. jaxarticum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒺藜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者虽为种下等级，但其原变种中文名即为“驼蹄瓣”，且“长果”正是其亚种加词</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">dolichocarpium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的直译，而</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jaxarticum </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">是地名，与“长果”字义无关，故前者保留原名。但马其云根据《植物志》所列别名将后者中文名改为“长果霸王”，并不合适。霸王是同科另一个属的中文名，“长果霸王”容易使人误以为按《植物志》的系统，该植物属于霸王属，因此不如新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">镰果驼蹄瓣</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，因其果镰形弯曲，是一特征。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">长轴杜鹃：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhododendron longistylum </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Rh.ramsdenianum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者的种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> longistylum </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">直译正是“长轴”，且该类群还有一个变种，名为“平卧长轴杜鹃”，而后者的种加词是人名，故保留前者原名。马其云改后者为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阮氏杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，可以采纳。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">川南野丁香：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Leptodermis handeliana </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">L.limprichtii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。二者都是狭域特有植物，前者分布于四川盐源，后者分布于四川天全。从实际地理位置上看，盐源位于川南，而天全位于川西而非川南，故前者保留原名，后者按马其云，径称“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">天全野丁香</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">大果杜鹃：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhododendron sinonuttallii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rh.glanduliferum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。马其云将前者改为“中国木兰杜鹃”，因其种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> sinonuttallii </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">系由</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> sino-</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（中国的）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> nuttallii </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">合成，而后者是木兰杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Rh. nuttallii </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的种加词，虽然很合理，但全名达六字，似嫌冗长。考虑到《图鉴》已将大果杜鹃作为前者的中文名，故前者应保留原名，后者新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">具腺杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，为其种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> glanduliferum </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的直译。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">大花杜鹃：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhododendron megalanthum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Rh. lindleyi</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者的种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">megalanthum </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">直译即为“大花”，故保留原名。马其云改后者为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">林氏杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，可以采纳。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">淡黄杜鹃：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhododendron flavidum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Rh. flavoflorum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者分布略广，且有种下等级，其种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">flavidum </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">直译即为“淡黄”，而后者分布十分局限，种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">flavoflorum </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的直译是“淡黄花”，故前者应保留原名，后者新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">淡黄花杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。马其云把前者改名为“川西淡黄杜鹃”是不太妥当的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">地锦：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Parthenocissus tricuspidata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葡萄科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Euphorbia humifusa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大戟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者的别名“爬山虎”广为人知，已成通称，因此对于这对重名来说，本以改前者为宜。但《植物志》葡萄科作者鉴于“地锦”见于《本草纲目》，为已知该植物最早名称，而选定此名作为其中文正名，且将其所在属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Parthenocissus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的中文名也定名为“地锦属”，同属其他植物也均以“地锦”为名，已不便更动，故只好将后者改名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">地锦草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(15)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">短苞薹草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Carex paxii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C.rubro-brunnea </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">brevibract</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者为种下等级，故改后者为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">短苞大理薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">对节刺：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Horaninowia ulicina</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sageratia pycnophylla</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鼠李科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Horaninowia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">亦以“对节刺”为名，故保留原名。马其云按《植物志》所记别名，改后者为“铁勒鞭棵棵”，这一土名既难记，又难以看出该植物所属的类群，故不取，新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">对刺雀梅藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，以表明该植物为雀梅藤属植物。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(17)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">风车草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cyperus alternfolius</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> subsp. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">flabelliformis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Clinopodium urticifolium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。《植物志》第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">67</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">分册上已经将后者更名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">麻叶风轮菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(18)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">高山薹草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Carex pseudo-supina</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C.infuscata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">gracilenta</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者为种下等级，故改名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">高山淡色薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(19)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">钩毛草属：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pseudechinolaena</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Kelloggia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二属重名。但因这二属在我国各只有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">种，</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pseudechinolaena</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ps.Polystachya</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中名“钩毛草”，</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Kelloggia </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">K. chinensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中名“云南钩毛草”，所以这一对属名重名未导致相应的种名重名。因《植物志》禾本科钩毛草属的编纂早于茜草科，且</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Kelloggia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">另有更准确的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">钩毛果</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">属”的中文名，故</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pseudechinolaena </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">保留原名，</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Kelloggia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">钩毛果属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">K.chinensis </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的中文名最好也改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">云南钩毛果</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，以求与属名对应。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(20)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">光萼蓝钟花：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cyananthus leiocalyx</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C.hookeri</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">levicalyx</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为桔梗科）重名。后者为种下等级，且该变种实际上茎、萼均光滑无毛，并非只有萼光滑无毛，所以虽然种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">levicalyx </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">是“光萼”之意，但并不准确，故保留前者原名，后者按马其云，改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">光蓝钟花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(21)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">光柱杜鹃：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhododendron tanastylum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Rh. flavidum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">psilostylum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者为种下等级，故改名为“光柱淡黄杜鹃”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(22)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">海仙花：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Weigela coraeensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">忍冬科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Primulapoissonii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">报春花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者在《植物志》上虽未正式立目，但现已成为广泛栽培的园艺花木，故保留原名，后者改用《图鉴》用过的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">海仙报春</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(23)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">红葱：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eleutherine plicata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸢尾科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Allium cepa </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">proliferum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">百合科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eleutherine</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">亦名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红葱属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故保留原名，而将后者按《植物志》所载异名改名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">楼子葱</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。实际上，因为后者伞形花序具大量珠芽，常常珠芽在花序上就发出幼叶，所以“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">楼子葱</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名本也比“红葱”更形象。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(24)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">红根草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Salvia prionitis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lysimachia fortunei</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">报春花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。由于《植物志》唇形科出版时间远早于报春花科，故前者保留原名。马其云按中药材名称改后者为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">星宿菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，这一名称可以和同属近缘的另两种</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">多育星宿菜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> L. prolifera</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">矮星宿菜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">L. pumila</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">相呼应，甚合适。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(25)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">虎尾草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Chloris virgata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lysimachia barystachys</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">报春花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Chloris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">亦名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虎尾草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故保留原名。后者本有“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">狼尾花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这一个广泛使用的名称，理应采纳。马其云改为“虎尾花”，此名不见于《植物志》，不知出自何处，不妥。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(26)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">黄兰：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cephalantheropsis gracilis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兰科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Michelia champaca</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木兰科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cephalantheropsis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">亦名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄兰属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故保留原名。对于后者，《植物志》记载了“黄玉兰”和“黄缅桂”两个中文异名，笔者认为均不合适。该植物属于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">含笑属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，而非木兰属，“黄玉兰”一名有误导之嫌；“缅桂”本是同属植物</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">白兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">M. alba</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）的中文异名，既然《植物志》选用了白兰而非缅桂作为该种中文名，</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">M. champaca</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">若再叫“黄缅桂”，就在同属植物中文名中找不到呼应，显得突兀。考虑到白兰一名白兰花，笔者建议新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄兰花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”作为</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">M.champaca </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的中文名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(27)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">黄钟花：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Stenolobium stans</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫葳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cyananthus flavus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桔梗科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者在《植物志》中虽然没有正式立目，仅在外来栽培植物检索表中出现。但是，因为该植物所在的</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Stenolobium </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">属我国仅引种</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">种，其中文名很容易被类推为“黄钟花属”，而同名桔梗科植物的分布十分局限，目前尚不知有何经济价值；且桔梗科植物的“黄钟花”一名系仿其属名“蓝钟花”而来，同属另有一种开白色花的植物</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C.montanus </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，又被叫做“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">白钟花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，只为了名副其实，就把这几个简洁明快的中文名同时用于一个属内的植物，无疑是很不经济的（而实际上，在颜色上名不副实的中文名是很多的，如紫茉莉的花就不都是紫色的，紫薇属的许多种更是从不开紫色花，却仍以“紫薇”为名）。故而，前者宜保留原名，后者按马其云改名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">丽江黄钟花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(28)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">火焰草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Castilleja pallida</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sedum stellariifolium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">景天科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属亦名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">火焰草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故保留原名。马其云改后者为“繁缕叶景天”，虽然更准确（其种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">stellariifolium </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">意即“叶似繁缕的”），但另有“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">繁缕景天</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名使用更广，也较为简洁，宜采用。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(29)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">鸡爪草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Calathodes oxycarpa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛茛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Orinus anomala</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Calathodes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">已经叫做“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸡爪草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故后者应改名。马其云拟为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">四川固沙草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，很合适。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(30)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">节节草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Equisetum ramosissimum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木贼科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Commelina diffusa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸭跖草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。马其云改前者为土木贼，后者保留节节草的原名，不妥。后者虽然在热带地区广布，但在我国分布很有限，而前者的分布则遍及全国，知名度较高。今保留前者的原名，后者改名竹节菜，为《植物志》记载的别名之一。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(31)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">金凤花：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Impatiens cyathiflora</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">凤仙花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Caesalpinia pulcherrima</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。《植物志》中前者未记别名，而后者记有三个别名，其中“洋金凤”且为广州地区通称。该植物非我国原产，名为“洋”甚当，故今从马其云，改后者为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">洋金凤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(32)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">金线草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Antenoron filiforme</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓼科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rubia membranacea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属已经叫“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">金线草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，所以应保留原名。后者改名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">金线茜草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，因其为茜草属植物。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(33)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蜡烛果：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Aegiceras corniculatum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫金牛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Parmentiera cerifera</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫葳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属已经叫“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蜡烛果属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，且是我国原产，所以应保留原名。后者为一引种栽培植物，新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蜡烛木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，其所在属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Parmentiera</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">可以拟名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蜡烛木属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。马其云分别拟名为“桐花树”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和“桐花树属”，实际上“桐花树”是前一种紫金牛科植物的别名，故不妥。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(34)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">狼毒：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Stellera chamaejasme</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瑞香科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Euphorbia fischeriana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大戟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属已经叫“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">狼毒属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故保留原名。后者已有“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">狼毒大戟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这一广泛使用的名称，理宜采之。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(35)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">林芝杜鹃：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhododendron nyingchiense </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rh. tanastylum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">lingzhiense</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者为种下等级，故保留前者原名。后者改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红点杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，为《植物志》所记别名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(36)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">龙头竹：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bambusa vulgaris </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Fargesiadracocephala</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者的种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">dracocephala </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">直译虽正是“龙头”，而且有一定的经济价值（在产区为大熊猫的主要采食竹种），但前者的两个栽培品种经济价值更大（均为南方常见观赏竹种）。而且《植物志》虽然在前者名下记了一个“泰山竹”的别名，但该竹绝不产于泰山，名不副实。故笔者不能苟同马其云将前者改名为“泰山竹”的做法。今为后者新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">龙头箭竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，以表明它是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">箭竹属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">植物。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(37)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">毛序棘豆：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oxytropis trichosphaera</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">O. trichophora</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。“毛序”是前者种加词的直译，故前者保留原名。马其云为后者新拟“毛状棘豆”，不妥。后者种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> trichophora </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> phora </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不是“……状的”，而是“具……的”之意，且“毛状”于语义也不通。故此处新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">具毛棘豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(38)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">帕米尔棘豆：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oxytropis gorbunovii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">O.poncinsii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。这二名的种加词俱为人名，且原均无中文名，均为《植物志》棘豆属作者所拟。马其云将前者改名为“中亚棘豆”，因《植物志》上记载前者的分布是“中亚（准噶尔阿拉套、天山、帕米尔－阿赖）也有分布”。实际上，从这一记载的括注来看，该种在中亚的分布其实很有限；而后者的国外分布，《植物志》记载为“哈萨克斯坦、乌兹别克斯坦、土库曼斯坦、吉尔吉斯斯坦和塔吉克斯坦”，而这正是中亚全部五个国家的名字，所以把后者拟名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">中亚棘豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”更合适。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(39)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">球菊：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Epaltes australis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bolocephalus saussureoides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名，同时</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Epaltes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bolocephalus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">二属也重名。前一属我国有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">种，</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">E.australis </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这一种又广布于我国南方热带地区，后者则为仅局限于我国西藏的单型属，故前者保留原名。马其云改后一种中文名为“毬菊”，实际上“毬”就是“球”的异体字，实际等于未改，而且按简化字规范也不应使用异体字，故不能采用。应俊生、张玉龙所著《中国种子植物特有属》一书上已为后一属新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">丝苞菊属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，宜采纳。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(40)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">三蕊草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sinochasea trigyna</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sonerila tenera</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">野牡丹科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属已名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">三蕊草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故保留原名。后者在《云南植物志》上叫“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">短药地胆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，马其云据此改之，甚合适。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(41)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">山慈姑（菇）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Iphigenia indica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">百合科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Asarum sagittarioides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马兜铃科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属已名为“山慈姑（菇）属”，故保留原名。后者在《图鉴》上叫“岩慈菇”，理应改为此名，但应该正字为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">岩慈姑</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”（详见下文第三节“正字”中“别字的订正”一段）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(42)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">山桂花：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bennettiodendron leprosipes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大风子科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Osmanthus delavayi</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木犀科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属已经叫“山桂花属”，故前者保留原名。后者《植物志》记有一个别名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">管花木犀</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”（出自《云南种子植物名录》），宜采用，但要改“犀”为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">樨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”（详见下文第三节“正字”中“异体字的订正”一段）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(43)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">珊瑚花：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cyrtanthera carnea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">爵床科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Jatropha multidifa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大戟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属已经叫“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">珊瑚花属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故前者保留原名。经在网上检索，后者又有“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红珊瑚</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的别名，今采以为新拟名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(44)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">水柳：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Homonoia riparia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大戟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Salixwarburgii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杨柳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属已经叫“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">水柳属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故前者保留原名。后者为台湾地方名，该种植物也是台湾特产，故新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">台湾水柳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(45)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">太白杜鹃：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhododendron taibaiense </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rh. purdomii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。马其云改前者为“太白山杜鹃”，只是多加了一个“山”字，实际等于未改名，故不妥。经查二者的分布，前者为太白山特有，后者则“产陕西西南部和东南部、甘肃南部和河南西部”，这几乎已经等于整个秦岭的范围，故新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">秦岭杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(46)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">铁马鞭：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lespedeza pilosa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhamnus aurea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鼠李科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。二者均为地方土名，但前者所在属中尚有一种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">L. fasciculiflora</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">名为“束花铁马鞭”，二名相互呼应，故宜按马其云，保留前者原名，而为后者新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">云南鼠李</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之名，以表明它是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鼠李属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">植物。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(47)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蜈蚣草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eremochloa ciliaris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pteris vittata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">凤尾蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属亦名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蜈蚣草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故前者保留原名，后者新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蜈蚣凤尾蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，以表明它是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">凤尾蕨属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">植物。不过需要指出的是，“蜈蚣草”作为后者的中文名已经广为人知，因此这里虽然按照“与科属名称相关的名称优先保留”的原则将后者改名，但将来若保留后者“蜈蚣草”之名，而将前者和前者所在属更名，可能更合理一些。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(48)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">喜马拉雅薹草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Carex nivalis </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> C.himalaica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者的种加词虽然就是“喜马拉雅”之意，但在《植物志》上仅为一存疑种而未正式立目，相反，前者是正式立目的，故前者保留原名，后者改名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">东喜马拉雅薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，因其产地记载为“西藏（察隅、墨脱、波密）”，均位于喜马拉雅山东段。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(49)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">细穗薹草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Carex tenuispicula</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C.longerostrata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">pallida</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者为种下等级，故改名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">细穗长嘴薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(50)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">虾子草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Mimulicalyx rosulatus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Nechamandra alternifolia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">水鳖科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名，同时</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Mimulicalyx</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Nechamandra</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">也重名。由于《植物志》玄参科编成时间远早于水鳖科，故前者保留原名。马其云改后一种和后一属为“水生草”“水生草属”，涵义太宽泛，不如吴征镒等在《植物志》第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷中使用的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虾子菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虾子菜属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”好。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(51)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">狭叶猪屎豆：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Crotalaria ochroleuca </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. linifolia </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">stenophylla</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者为种下等级，故按马其云，改为“狭线叶猪屎豆”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(52)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">小叶地锦：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Parthenocissus chinensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葡萄科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Euphorbiaheyneana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大戟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者保留原名（原因见上文对“地锦”一名的讨论）。马其云将后者改名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">闽南大戟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，并在《中国蕨类植物和种子植物名称总汇》一书的“前言与使用说明”中，称该植物原有此别名，故从之。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(53)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">小叶散爵床：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rostellularia diffusa </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和其种下等级</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> R. d. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">prostrata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">爵床科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。显然前者应该保留原名。马其云改后者中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">平卧爵床</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，很合适，因其变种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> prostrata </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">意即“平卧的”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(54)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">小羽贯众：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cyrtomium lonchitoides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C.fortunei f. polypterum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鳞毛蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者为种下等级，马其云改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">多羽贯众</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，符合其变型加词意义，故采之。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(55)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">斜叶榕：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ficus tinctoria</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和其种下等级</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">F.t. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">gibbosa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桑科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。虽然后者为一亚种，但在我国的分布远较原变种广，因此宜保留原名。经在网上查询，该植物原亚种在台湾有“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山猪枷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的土名，可以采作新拟名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(56)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">锈点薹草：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Carex pseudo-ligulata </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. setosa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">punctata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span
