style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者为种下等级，改名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">锈点刺毛薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(57)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">锈红杜鹃：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhododendron complexum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rh.bureavii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。二种在云南均有分布，在《云南植物志》上，前者名为“锈红杜鹃”，后者名为“锈红毛杜鹃”，并不相同，而《植物志》将后者中文名也改为“锈红杜鹃”，才出现重名。今仍从《云南植物志》，恢复后者“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">锈红毛杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(58)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">岩参：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cicerbita azurea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Piper pubicatulum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">胡椒科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属已名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">岩参属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，且后者虽然可入药，但药用部分为茎而非根，叫“参”并不合适，故保留前者原名。马其云为后者新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">岩椒</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名，既去掉了名不副实的“参”字，又保留了描述其攀附于石壁上的习性的“岩”字，“椒”字又取自其属名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">胡椒属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，一箭三雕，甚妙。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(59)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">野百合：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lilium brownii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">百合科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属即名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">百合属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，而后者所在属是猪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">屎豆属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，《植物志》上全属仅此一种名</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Crotalaria sessiliflora</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字带“百合”二字，理应改名。但马其云起用的“紫花野百合”一名，却不合适，因为这样还是在一个和百合属不相关的属中保留了一个叫“百合”的中文名，容易使人误解。事实上，该种另有一个叫“农吉利”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的别名广为人知（《植物志》也收载了），从该植物中提取的“农吉利碱”是著名药物，在《中华人民共和国药典》中该药即是以此名为正名收载的，故其原植物定名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">农吉利</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”最合适不过。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(60)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">野牡丹：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Melastoma candidum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">野牡丹科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Paeonia delavayi</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛茛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。“野牡丹”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">一名不仅用来命名了前者所在的属，还用来命名了前者所在的科，且马其云已指出，该名在清代徐葆光所著《中山传信录》中已应用于前者，故前者理所当然应该保留原名。正好《植物志》记载后者有一别名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫牡丹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，起用之即可解决问题。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(61)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">野苏子：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis grandiflora</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Elsholtzia flava</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。《植物志》第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">67</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">分册已将后者改名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄花香薷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(62)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">隐脉杜鹃：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhododendron maddenii </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rh. subenerve</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。马其云因后者种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">subenerve</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">含义即为“隐脉”，而将前者改为“马登杜鹃”，不妥。前者不仅较多见，而且是其所在组的模式，因此该组的中文名也沿用了“隐脉杜鹃”一名，而后者《植物志》注明“未见标本”。故前者保留原名，后者新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">灌阳杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，灌阳是广西东北部县名，为其模式标本产地。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(63)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">硬毛棘豆：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oxytropis hirta</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">O.fetissovii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者分布远较后者广泛，且其所在亚属的中文名也被拟为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">硬毛棘豆亚属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。《植物志》棘豆属作者虽然将后者所在的亚组的中文名也拟为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">硬毛棘豆亚组</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，但这个“硬毛”来自亚组名</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">O.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Subsect. Hirsutae</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，而和其学名无干，且该植物在我国仅分布于新疆西北一隅，因此保留</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">O. hirta</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的原名为妥。马其云把前者改名为“毛棘豆”，是不太合适的。今为后一植物新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">糙硬毛棘豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，其亚组中文名也可以相应改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">糙硬毛棘豆亚组</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，最大程度地照顾到了其原名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(64)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">玉树杜鹃：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhododendron yushuense </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rh. przewalskii </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">yushuense</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为杜鹃花科）重名。后者为种下等级，故前者保留原名。但后者如拟名为“玉树陇蜀杜鹃”则不妥，因为这种两个二字地名的重复修饰不合汉语习惯（详见下文第二节“和种下等级有关的中文名订正”中“由种下等级旧命名法所得中文名的订正”一段），故新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">囊谦杜鹃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，囊谦为青海县名，为其模式标本产地（《植物志》记载其模式标本产地为昂欠，昂欠是“囊谦”的另一音译，不符合地名标准化规范，宜废）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(65)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">圆叶报春：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Primula baileyana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">P.vaginata </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">encyclia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">报春花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。后者为种下等级，故改名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">圆叶鞘柄报春</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(66)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">掌叶木：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Handeliodendron bodinieri</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">无患子科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Tabebuia rosea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫葳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）重名。前者所在属已被命名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">掌叶木属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，为我国原产，《植物志》正式立目，后者仅为一外来栽培植物，《植物志》未正式立目，故前者保留原名。后者同属另一种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">T.chrysantha</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">我国亦有栽培，《植物志》名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄钟木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故后者可拟名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">红花黄钟木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，“红花”是其种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> rosea </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的意译。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">综上所述，在马其云总结的三条原则的基础上，改重名的原则可以进一步概括为以下几条：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">与种上等级（主要是科属，有时也包括属下种上的组、亚组等）相关的中文名优先保留；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">种级类群的名称比种下等级类群的中文名优先保留；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">应用时间长的中文名（如《植物志》早出版的卷册上的中文正名）优先保留；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">由影响力较大的专著使用过的中文名优先保留；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">分布较广、经济价值较大的类群的中文名优先保留；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">如果一个种或种下等级的中文名和所在属的中文名无关，而这一中文名的中心语（如上述大戟属“小叶地锦”中的“地锦”）在同属其他植物中文名中也有应用，则因改名会破坏这几个中文名原本的呼应关系，故优先保留原名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">对不保留原名的类群的改名方法，也可以更准确地表述为以下三条：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">可以从原有别名中选一个尚未被其他植物应用的名称作为正名，但不建议使用过长、不准确或看不出所在科属的名字；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">新拟名称时，最好以属名为基础，冠以种加词的中文对译、植物形态特征或出产地名等修饰语（即所谓“中文加词”，下文第二节“和种下等级有关的中文名订正”中还要详细讨论这个概念），修饰语务求简洁、准确；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">种下等级类群的中文名可以由一个上述类型的修饰语加种中文名构成。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">当然，在实际应用时，这些原则有时会发生冲突，这时候就要具体分析、灵活处理了。总之，一切以便于应用、影响最小为标准。</span></p><p style="text-align:left;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"><br  /></span></p><h1 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:7px;"><span style="font-family:宋体;">二、和种下等级有关的中文名订正</span></h1><h2 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;">1. <span style="font-family:宋体;">种和自动名中文名不匹配的订正：</span></h2><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">按</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">ICBN</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如果要在一个种下面建立种下等级，则自动建立原种下等级的自动名，这个自动名中的种下等级加词是和种加词相同的，如在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄荆</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Vitex negundo</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马鞭草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）下建立变种时，就自动生成一个</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">Vitexnegundo </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">negundo</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的自动名。不过，在自动名是否立目上，《植物志》各卷并不统一。早期的卷册往往不立目，后来的卷册则均立目。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">上文“引言”中已述，这种自动名的中文名应该是和种中文名相同的，若有意区别，至多是在后面括注“原亚种”、“原变种”等字样。《植物志》中绝大多数情况都是这样的。但是，也有个别种的自动名和种中文名不一致；或者如因原种下等级我国不产，而未给自动名立目时，种中文名和其种下等级中文名相同，这就意味着自动名的中文名就无法和种中文名相同了。下面就对属于这两种情况的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">16</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个中文名作一订正（按种中文名原名的音序排列）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">凹叶球兰</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Hoyaobovata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">萝藦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">原变种产印度尼西亚。《植物志》把种中文名和产于我国的变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">H. o.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">kerrii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">都叫做“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">凹叶球兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，造成自动名无法和种中文名相同。今为种新拟中文名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">倒卵叶球兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，“倒卵叶”为其种加词的意译。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">腹水草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Veronicastrum stenostachyum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">原亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">V. s. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">stenostachyum </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">V.s. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> plukenetii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">我国均产。《植物志》中前者名为“细穗腹水草”，后者名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">腹水草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”；又因后者分布更广泛，而把种中文名叫做“腹水草”，这是不妥的。种中文名应和原亚种中文名相同，均叫“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">细穗腹水草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">甘蓝</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Brassicaoleracea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">十字花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">原变种为英国及地中海地区野生，《植物志》称之“野甘蓝”，但种中文名却和变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> B. o. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. <em>capitata </em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">相同，故种中文名宜改作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">野甘蓝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">金钱豹</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Campanumoeajavanica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桔梗科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">情况同上，原亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. j. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">javanica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大花金钱豹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> C. j.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> subsp.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> japonica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">金钱豹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）我国均产。种中文名宜作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大花金钱豹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">聚花风铃草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Campanulaglomerata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桔梗科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">情况亦同。原亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. g.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> subsp. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">glomerata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">北疆风铃草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. g. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">cephalotes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">聚花风铃草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）我国均产。种中文名宜作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">北疆风铃草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">柳穿鱼</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Linaria vulgaris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">我国仅产</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">L. v. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> sinensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">L. v.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> subsp. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">acutiloba</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">二亚种。《植物志》把前者和种均叫“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柳穿鱼</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，今为种新拟中文名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">欧洲柳穿鱼</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">茅膏菜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Drosera peltata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茅膏菜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">《植物志》记载了产于我国的两个变种，其中</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">D.p. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">multisepala</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茅膏菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。今为种新拟中文名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">盾叶茅膏菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，“盾叶”为其种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> peltata </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的意译。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">南苜蓿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Medicago polymorpha</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">《植物志》非正式地记载了本种的三个变种（包括原变种），称我国常见的标本大都属于</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">M. p.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">vulgaris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。虽然苜蓿属的作者说：“其他两个变种也偶见有类似的标本。但标本的变化较大，一般不再作变种处理。”但他并没有正式将非原变种的两个变种归并。这样一来，与其保留种中文名原名，使分布最广的变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">M. p. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">vulgaris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不得不另拟名，不如将“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">南苜蓿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这一名字给了这个分布最广的变种，而为种和原变种再拟新名，以尽量减少混乱。笔者拟为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">多型苜蓿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，“多型”为其种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> polymorpha </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的直译。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">球花脚骨脆</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Casearia glomerata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大风子科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">其种中文名在《植物志》中为“球花脚骨脆”，但原变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. g. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">glomerata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">却叫“球果脚骨脆”。后者可能是印刷错误，应正为和种中文名相同的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">球花脚骨脆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">全缘凤丫蕨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Coniogrammefraxinea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">裸子蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">《植物志》为其自动名</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. f.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> f. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">fraxinea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">起名为“有齿凤丫蕨”，变型起名为“微齿凤丫蕨”，均与种中文名不同。其原变型羽片边缘全缘，并没有齿，因此其原变型的中文名仍应叫“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">全缘凤丫蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，“有齿凤丫蕨”应作为中文异名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">水珠草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Circaealutetiana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柳叶菜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">原亚种产于欧洲、非洲北部和亚洲西南部。《植物志》把种中文名和产于我国的亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C.l. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">quadrisulcata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">都叫作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">水珠草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。今为种中文名新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">欧洲水珠草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">太平山冬青</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Ilex sugeroklii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">冬青科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">《植物志》上，种中文名、原变种和变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">I. s.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> brevipedunculata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">三者同名。今为种中文名和原变种新拟“长梗太平山冬青”，因原变种的果梗较长。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">兔尾状黄耆</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Astragaluslaguroides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">《植物志》上的种中文名为“兔尾状黄耆”，原变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">A. l. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">laguroides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">则名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兔尾黄耆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，另一变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">A. l.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">micranthus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小花兔尾黄耆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。显然“兔尾黄耆”比“兔尾状黄耆”简洁，故种中文名应更名，同时改“耆”为“芪”（详见下文第三节“正字”中“异体字的订正”一段）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">椭圆叶花锚</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Haleniaelliptica </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">elliptica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">龙胆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">《植物志》管种中文名叫“椭圆叶花锚”，原变种却叫“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">卵萼花锚</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。该植物的叶形实际变化较大，并不均为椭圆形，而萼片的形状变异相对较小，故“卵萼花锚”一名更恰当，宜保留，而将“椭圆叶花锚”作为中文异名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(15</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">锡生藤</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cissampelospareira</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">防己科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">原变种分布美洲热带和非洲热带。《植物志》把种中文名和产于我国的变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. p.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">hirtusa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">均叫做“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">锡生藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，且未为原变种拟名，故在此新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">美非锡生藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”作为其种中文名和原变种的名字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">硬叶兰</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cymbidiumbicolor</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兰科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">原亚种产印度南部和斯里兰卡。《植物志》把种中文名和产于我国的亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> C. b. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">obtusum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">都叫做“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">硬叶兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，其种中文名理应和自动名中文名相同，均作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">南亚硬叶兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><h2 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;">2.<span style="font-family:宋体;">由种下等级旧命名法所得中文名的订正：</span></h2><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">以上的订正，都涉及种下等级中文名和种中文名的关系。还有一种需要订正的情况是和种下等级本身的命名方法有关的。《植物志》上对种下等级的中文命名，有四种方法。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">第一种是采用不包含属名也不包含种中文名的俗名</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瓠子</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lagenaria siceraria</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">hispida</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瓠瓜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> L. s. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">depressa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（属中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，种中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">第二种是“单一修饰语＋中心语”的结构</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，又可以再细分为五种情况：</span></p><p style="margin-left:56px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">一是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">种下等级为“单一修饰语＋属中文名”，而种中文名是不同于属名的俗名</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">英德羊蹄甲</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bauhiniachampionii </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> yingtakensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（属中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">羊蹄甲属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，种中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">龙须藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）；</span></p><p style="margin-left:56px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">二是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">种下等级和种中文名都是“单一修饰语＋属中文名”的结构，只是修饰语不同</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">百花山柴胡</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bupleurum chinense</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> f.<em> octoradiatum</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（属中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柴胡属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，种中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">北柴胡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）；</span></p><p style="margin-left:56px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">三是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">种下等级和种中文名都是“单一修饰语＋中心语”的结构，但这个中心语不同于属名</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小苞雪莲</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Saussurea pubifolia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>lhasaensis</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（属中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">风毛菊属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，种中文名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛背雪莲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）；</span></p><p style="margin-left:56px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">四是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">种中文名为不同于属名的俗名，而种下等级是“单一修饰语＋种中文名”的结构</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛叶老鸦糊</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Callicarpa giraldii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>lyi</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（属中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫珠属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，种中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">老鸦糊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）；</span></p><p style="margin-left:56px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">五是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">种中文名即属名，种下等级是“单一修饰语＋属名（种中文名）”的结构</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">念珠薏苡</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Coix lacryma-jobi </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em> maxima</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（属中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薏苡属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，种中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薏苡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">不管哪一种情况，这种种下等级中文名中的单一修饰语都大致可以和双名法中的加词相比，而且其意义往往也来自其种下加词，因此不妨称之为“中文加词”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">第三种是“第一个中文加词＋第二个中文加词＋中心语”的结构</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，这时候，中心语往往就是属名，而“第二个中文加词＋中心语”往往就是种中文名，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">多裂腺毛蝇子草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Silene yetii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>herbilegorum</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（属中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蝇子草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，种中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">腺毛蝇子草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">第四种是“种中文名＋中文加词＋变种”（或“亚种”、“变型”）的结构</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">头花马先蒿四川变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis cephalantha</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>szetchuanica</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（种中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">头花马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）。这种结构的名字集中见于个别出较比较早的卷册，包括第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">36</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">65</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">分册和第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">66</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">67</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">分册和第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">68</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">74</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷和第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">75</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），仅少数散见于其他卷册。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">无疑，现在使用最多的种下等级中文名，是用前三种方法命名的，其中又以第二种为多。第四种命名方法是已经淘汰、不再使用的命名方法。之所以这种命名方法被淘汰，首先是因为由此得到的种下等级中文名太长，如《植物志》中最长的四个名字（长达</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">17</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字）均是用这种方法命名的（如“</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#47C1A8;">碎米蕨叶马先蒿碎</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">米蕨叶亚种等唇变种</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）；但更重要的是，随着研究的不断深入，植物类群的分类地位是常常在变动中的，一旦种下等级发生变动，这种中文名势必也要改变，由此就造成中文名的不稳定性，不利应用和交流。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">因此，对这种类型的种下等级中文名进行订正，就很有必要。马其云在《总汇》一书中已经将全部这种类型的中文名做了订正，其订正方法可以总结为两条：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">把原名中的中文加词提到种中文名前，去掉“变种”“亚种”“变型”字样</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如上述头花马先蒿四川变种，就订正为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">四川头花马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">如果原名中有来自学名自动名的部分，就把这部分也去掉</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如上述“碎米蕨叶马先蒿碎米蕨叶亚种等唇变种”中，“碎米蕨叶亚种”对应的是其学名中的自动</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">名，故这六字全删，原名订正为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">等唇碎米蕨叶马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">在这一基础上，笔者再提出第三条：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">如果原名中包含学名中两个不同的种下等级的对应部分，就只保留最低一个种下等级对应部分的中文加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如“寸金草披针叶变种近无毛变型”，订正为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">近无毛寸金草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，而不是“近无毛披针叶寸金草”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这样得到的订正后的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">700</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">多个名字，大部分属于上述第三种命名法。事实上，按现在通行的命名法，原名中的种中文名如果也是“中文加词＋中心语”的结构，则连这个中文加词都可以去掉，而使该种下等级中文名成为第二种命名法命名的名字，如上述“等唇碎米蕨叶马先蒿”便可以进一步简为“等唇马先蒿”。但是这样会造成大量的重名，如“四川头花马先蒿”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">若简为“四川马先蒿”，就和同属另一种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis szetschuanica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的中文名重名了。若笔者为此拟定许多新名称，则有悖于修订《植物志》中文名的初衷。所以，为统一起见，虽然有的种下等级已经有十分通行的第二类命名法的名字，但笔者并不采用，仍按上述订正方法进行订正；如毛叶香茶菜蓝萼变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rabdosia japonica </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em>glaucocalyx</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（唇形科），虽然在许多华北地区的地方植物志上都简作“蓝萼香茶菜”，但笔者订正为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓝萼毛叶香茶菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，其中“毛叶”二字并不省略。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">只有在下列几种情况下，笔者才新拟第二类命名法的名字，这些情况包括：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">订正所得的名字中的两个中文加词互相矛盾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（如“绿柄红柄白鹃梅”）</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">或文字累赘</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（如“极弱弱小马先蒿”）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">订正所得的名字中的两个中文加词都是地名或人名，而不合汉语习惯</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（如“建德杭州石荠苎”）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">订正所得的名字和已有的中文名重名</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（如“脓疮草小花变种”如订正为“小花脓疮草”则与同属另一种重名）；</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">订正后的名字仍然太长</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（如“二回羽状边缘鳞盖蕨”，长达</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">9</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">好在这种新拟的名字并不多，只有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">29</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个，下面按原名的音序一一罗列：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">边缘鳞盖蕨二回羽状变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Microlepia marginata </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em>bipinnata</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">碗蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">上文已述，若订正为“二回羽状边缘鳞盖蕨”，名字仍嫌太长。新拟“二羽边缘鳞盖蕨”，因同属另有一种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">M. bipinnata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">二羽鳞盖蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，是其先例。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">苍山糙苏独龙变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Phlomis forrestii </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em>taronensis</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">地名重叠，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">独龙糙苏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">长叶火绒草短叶变型</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Leontopodium longifolium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> f.<em>brevifolium</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中文加词矛盾，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">短叶火绒草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">淡黄香青淡红变型</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Anaphalis flavescens</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> f. <em>rosea</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中文加词矛盾，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">淡红香青</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">淡黄香青硫黄变型</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">A. f.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> f.<em>sulphrea</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">同上</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中文加词矛盾，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">硫黄香青</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">滇池海棠川鄂变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Malus yunnanensis </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em>veitchii</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">地名重叠，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">川鄂海棠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">钝齿花楸锐齿变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sorbus helenae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>argutiserrata</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中文加词矛盾。但若简作“锐齿花楸”，又和同属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> S. arguta</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的中文名重名，故新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">川西花楸</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，因其产于四川西部。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">甘菊甘野菊变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Dendranthema lavandulifolium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>seticuspe</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">文字累赘。事实上“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">甘野菊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”就是该种下等级一个很好的第一类命名法的名字，直接起用即可。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">甘肃马先蒿青海亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis kansuensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> subsp.<em>kokonorica</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">地名重叠，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">青海马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">灌木紫菀木无舌状花变型</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Asterothamnus fruticosus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> f.<em>discoideus</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">若订正为“无舌状花灌木紫菀木”，名字嫌太长，新拟“隐舌灌木紫菀木”，“隐舌”一名可见于同科植物“隐舌橐吾”</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ligularia franchetiana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">杭州石荠苎建德变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Mosla hangchowensis </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. <em>cheteana</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">地名重叠，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">建德石荠苎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">黑花糙苏狭叶变种浅色变型</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Phlomis melanantha </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em>angustifolia</em> f.<em> pallidior</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">若订正为“浅色黑花糙苏”，则与另一种下等级</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Ph. m.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> f.<em>pallidior </em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">订正后的中文名重名（其原名为“黑花糙苏浅色变型”），故其中文名应作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">浅色狭叶黑花糙苏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，“狭叶”二字不能省。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">红柄白鹃梅绿柄变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Exochorda giraldii </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em> wilsonii</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中文加词矛盾，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绿柄白鹃梅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">红花来江藤黄花变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Brandisia rosea </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em> flava</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中文加词矛盾，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄花来江藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(15)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">黄山鼠尾草婺源变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Salvia chienii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em> wuyuania</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">地名重叠，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">婺源鼠尾草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">金江火把花沧江变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Colquhounia compta </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em> mekongensis</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">地名重叠，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">沧江火把花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(17)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">京黄芩黑龙江变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Scutellaria pekinensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>ussuriensis</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">地名重叠，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黑龙江黄芩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(18)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">吕宋黄芩乐东变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">S. luzonica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>lotungensis</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（同上）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">地名重叠，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">乐东黄芩</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(19)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">罗氏马先蒿萧氏亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis roylei </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp. <em>shawii</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">人名重叠，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">萧氏马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(20)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">脓疮草小花变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Panzeria alaschanica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>minor</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">同属已有</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">P. parviflora</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小花脓疮草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小脓疮草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，因其变种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">minor </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">直译即“较小的”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(21)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">铺散马先蒿高升亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis diffusa </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp.<em>elatior</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中文加词矛盾，但若简作“高升马先蒿”，又和同属另一种</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">P. elata </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">重名，故新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">较高升马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，因其亚种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> elatior </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> elata </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的比较级，意即“较高升的”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(22)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">全叶马先蒿全缘亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">P. integrifolia </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp.<em>integerrima</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（同上）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">文字累赘，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">全缘马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(23)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">弱小马先蒿极弱亚种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">P. debilis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> subsp.<em>debilior</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（同上）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">文字累赘，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">极弱马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(24)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">深紫糙苏浅紫变型</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Phlomis atropurpurea </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">f.<em>pallidior</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中文加词矛盾，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">浅紫糙苏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(25)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">石楠窄叶变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Photinia serrulata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>ardisiifolia</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">同属已有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Ph. Stenophylla </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的中文名为“窄叶石楠”，故新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫金牛叶石楠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，是其变种加词的直译。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(26)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">鼠尾草翅柄变型</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Salvia japonica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> f.<em>alatopinnata</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">同属已有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> S. alatipetiolata </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的中文名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">翅柄鼠尾草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，故新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">延翅鼠尾草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，“延翅”这一中文加词可见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">延翅风毛菊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">延翅蛇根草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”等名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(27)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">四川香茶菜永胜变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rabdosia setschwanensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>yungshengensis</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">地名重叠，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">永胜香茶菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(28)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">狭盔马先蒿狭盔亚种极狭变种</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis stenocorys </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">subsp. <em>stenocorys</em>var.<em> angustissima</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">文字累赘，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">极狭马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(29)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">腺梗豨莶无腺变型</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Siegesbeckia pubescens</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> f.<em>eglandulosa</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中文加词矛盾，故简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">无腺豨莶</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-align:left;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span></p><h1 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;"><span style="font-family:宋体;">三、正字</span></h1><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">按照现代汉语的用字规范，《植物志》中有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">5</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个科中文名、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">44</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个属中文名和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1200</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">多个种中文名的用字需要订正。这有如下几个情况：</span></p><h2 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;">1.<span style="font-family:宋体;">改掉少数民族的旧称：</span></h2><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">众所周知，我国有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">55</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个少数民族，有不少少数民族在历史上有多个称呼，建国后则为每个少数民族固定了唯一的称呼。使用这唯一的名称，是对少数民族的尊重，因此即使有的旧称可能字面上并无贬意，继续使用也不合适。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">植物志中有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">17</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个名称的订正属于这种情况。其中</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">15</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个使用了“俅（求）江”的字样，如俅江龙胆、俅江紫堇、求江蔷薇等。俅江是独龙江的旧称，居住在其流域的俅人，现名独龙族。这</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">15</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个名称中的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">俅（求）江”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">均应改作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">独龙江”；仅俅江紫堇</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Corydalis kiukiangensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">罂粟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）若改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">独龙江紫堇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，则与同属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. dulongjiangensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中文名相重，可以新拟“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">贡山紫堇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，因其模式标本采自贡山（为云南西北部县名）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">另两个名称中，一个是傜山稀子蕨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Monachosorum elegens</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">稀子蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），应改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">瑶山稀子蕨</span><span
