style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”；另一个是回回苏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Perillafrutescens var. crispa</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。《植物志》中另有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茴茴蒜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ranunculus chinensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛茛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），其中的“茴”字本也是“回”的别字。按理说，别字是应该改正的，但是如将“茴茴蒜”正为“回回蒜”，就等于重新使用了“回回”这个回族的旧称。由于涉及到民族问题，改掉少数民族的旧称应该优先于改正别字，所以“茴茴蒜”中的“茴”字不宜恢复为“回”字。反过来，“回回苏”可以改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茴茴苏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，从而回避掉对“回回”的直接使用。</span></p><h2 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;">2.<span style="font-family:宋体;">改掉部分</span> GBK <span style="font-family:宋体;">字库中未收录的冷僻字：</span></h2><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库是现在中文操作系统使用最广泛的字库，共收字</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">万余个，已经能够满足大部分的应用需求。《植物志》收载的植物中文正名共用字</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2400</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">多个，大部分</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库均收录，只有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">12</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个冷僻字是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库所没有的。尽管现在又有更新的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GB18030</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库，收字更多，以后还能不断扩展，但并不是所有的软件都支持（目前仅在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Office2003</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等软件中可用），而且植物中文名为便于应用，应该具有易读、易写、易记的特点，所以即使将来技术的进步可以解决更多汉字的输入和存储问题，植物中文名中的冷僻字仍是越少越好。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">下面将这</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">12</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个字用描述法列出（无符号表示左右结构，“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”表示上下结构，“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">@</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”表示半包围结构），并作简单考证。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">杭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">子梢属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Campylotropis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为豆科属名。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">杭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字很显然是后起字，其本字和本义待考。这个字《现代汉语词典》第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">5</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">版（以下简称《现汉》）和《中华大字典》均未收入，其读音莫衷一是，即使不考虑声调，也有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> hang </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> kang </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">两种念法。但在植物学界，以念</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> kang </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为多，如《总汇》和傅立国主编的《中国高等植物》中均将此字按</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> kang </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的读音编入检索表。查《现汉》，以“亢”为偏旁而音节为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> kang </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的字中，大多数读去声，仅“闶”和“忼”两字读阴平，且前者只出现在方言词汇中，后者是“慷”的异体字。故笔者建议</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">杭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">] </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> kang4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">杭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">子梢属在我国广布，此字不宜废除，但可惜的是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GB18030</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库仍未收录。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">䓫</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">䓫</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">莱主山，为台湾玉山山脉南段一高峰。以这一命名的植物有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">䓫莱乌头</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Aconitum bartlettii</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛茛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。另一种奇莱红门兰</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Orchis kiraishiensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兰科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的奇也应作</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">䓫</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。地名使用的冷僻字，一般来说是不宜废除的，除非另拟名。此字</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GB18030</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库已收。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;color:#FFA000;">𫈰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> qia4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;color:#5B9BD5;">𫈰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Koeleria</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">属名。此字《现汉》已收，故不宜废除，但</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GB18030</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库未收。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">豆劳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> lao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆劳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Glycine soja</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科大豆属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">植物。此字本作</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，《玉篇》《广韵》均收有此字。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">豆劳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">是后起字，“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">豆劳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">豆”一名见于明朱橚《救荒本草》。豆科大豆属作者以为《救荒本草》是记载该植物的最早文献，出于“用文献最早记载的名称作为中文正名”的原则选用了“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">豆劳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">豆”的名称，不仅于实不符，而且白白增加了一个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">GB18030</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库也未收入的冷僻字。实际上，此种广泛分布于全国，且是国家二级保护植物，通称野大豆，故不如仍定名为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">野大豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，以免冷僻字之烦。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">㟖</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> long4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。据《现汉》，此字是壮语的音译，意为“山间的小块平地”，大量出现于广西地名中。㟖岗原为广西龙州县村名，后来在此建立㟖岗国家级自然保护区，为不少植物的模式标本采集地。以“㟖岗”或“弄岗”为名的植物有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">8</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">种（含</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">变种），如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">㟖岗耳叶马蓝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">㟖岗唇柱苣苔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">㟖岗轮环藤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等（其中弄岗马兜铃、弄岗金花茶、弄岗黄皮应正字为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">㟖岗马兜铃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”、“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">㟖岗金花茶</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”、“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">㟖岗黄皮</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）。且此字在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GB18030</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中已经收录，故不宜废除</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">沙</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> sha1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">沙</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">簕竹</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Schizostachyum diffusum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;color:#5B9BD5;">𥯨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">簩竹属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">植物，分布于我国台湾和菲律宾。“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">沙</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">簕”是台湾地方名，其义不详，可能源于高山语。此冷僻字在《植物志》中仅出现一次，“簕”字虽然出现多次，但在这里仅仅是记音而并未用其本义（关于其本义的分析详见下文），故宜改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">沙勒竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;color:#FFA000;">𥯨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> si1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;color:#5B9BD5;">𥯨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">簩竹</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Schizostachyum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">属名。此名最早见于西晋嵇含《南方草木状》，且现已用为属名，不宜废除。此字</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GB18030</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库未收。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">闾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> l</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">ü</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。菴</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">闾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">]</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Artemisia keiskeana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科蒿属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">植物。《本草纲目•草部第十五卷》对这个名字的解释是：“菴，草屋也。闾，里门也。此草乃蒿属，老茎可以盖覆菴闾，故以名之。”这样说来，菴不过是庵的异体，而</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">闾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">则是从闾字生造来的。因此，虽然</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GB18030</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库已经收录了此字，此名仍以订正为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">庵闾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”为宜。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">㼎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马㼎儿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Zehner</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">属名。葫芦科另有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">赤瓟属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Thladiantha</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄瓜属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">还有叫</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">小马泡</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cucumis bisexualis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">马泡瓜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">C. melo var. agrestis</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的两种植物，这里的㼎、瓟和泡实际上都是一个字，应该统一。其中，泡是别字（详见下文“别字的订正”一段），而在㼎和瓟两字中，《现汉》收了前者。鉴此，此字不仅不应废除，连赤瓟属的“瓟”字和小马泡、马泡瓜中的“泡”字也应订正为此字。好在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GB18030</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中已经收录了㼎。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">月君</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jun1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。鸡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">月君</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">梅花草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Parnassia wightiana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为虎耳草科梅花草属植物。此字（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">GB18030</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库未收）实际上是“肫”（读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zhun1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）的方言读音，两字意义无别，都是指鸟类的胃，故宜将此植物名改为鸡肫梅花草。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">䉡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> dan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。木䉡竹</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bambusa wenchouensis </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科簕竹属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">植物。此名见于元李衎《竹谱详录》，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">䉡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">竹实际上就是“单竹”的异写，故宜将此植物名改为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木单竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（虽然此字</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GB18030</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库已收）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;color:#FFA000;">𣐿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yi1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。栘（读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:SimSun-ExtB;">𣐿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Docynia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">为蔷薇科属名。《现汉》收录了此字，故不宜废除，但</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GB18030</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库未收。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">综上所述，这</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">12</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个冷僻字中，笔者建议</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">废除</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">豆劳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">沙</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">闾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">月君</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">竹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">亶</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">]5</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">个字</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。另</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">7</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个则应暂时保留。</span></p><h2 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;">3.<span style="font-family:宋体;">异体字的订正：</span></h2><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">由于传统沿袭，《植物志》收载的中文正名中，有许多异体字，甚至有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">25</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个属的属名也包含有异体字。有的含异体字的属名如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">木犀属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">杓兰属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蛾眉蕨属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">使用十分广泛，要改变人们长期养成的用字习惯，殊为不易。但是，为了汉语的规范性，按《现汉》的规定改正这些异体字，仍是一件有必要的事情。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">下面一一对这些异体字做介绍：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">属中文名和种（含种下等级）中文名中都包含的异体字有（按音序排列，举属中文名以赅该属中种中文名）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">瓟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">赤瓟属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的瓟应改为㼎，已见上“改掉部分</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">未收录的冷僻字”一段。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蒭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中无简化字。它是刍的异体字，故</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蒭雷草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Thuarea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）应改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">刍雷草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蛾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蛾眉蕨属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lunathyrium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蹄盖蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的蛾字，正作“娥”。但</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">飞蛾藤属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Porana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">旋花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">飞蛾槭</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Acer oblongum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">槭树科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的蛾字不改。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蕃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在作“来自国外的”解时，这个字是“番”的异体。因此</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泽蕃椒属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Deinostemma</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（玄参科）应正作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">泽番椒</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">疯</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">麻疯树属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Jatropha</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（大戟科）中的疯字，正作“风”。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山麻风树</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Turpinia pomifera</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">省沽油科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）的写法是正确的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">桿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字是杆的异体字。但</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">膜蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的两个属，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">球桿毛蕨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Nesopteris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">毛桿蕨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Callistropteris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中的桿字应该正作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">秆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”（详见下文“别字的订正”一段）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">桔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：桔字仅在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桔梗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”一名中为正体，而且读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> jie2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其他情况下都是橘（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">ju2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）的异体字（或曰俗体字）。黄成就在《植物志》芸香科一卷中对桔橘二字的关系做了很好的解释，他主编的这一卷就绝未使用一个“桔”字，但在其他卷册中，以桔代橘的情况屡有发生，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">越桔属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Vaccinium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（杜鹃花科），及种名</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">桔红山楂</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">越桔叶蔓榕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">越桔叶忍冬</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">假金桔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。这些名字中的桔均应正作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">橘</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">脈</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：为脉的异体字。此异体字仅见于《植物志》出版最早的第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷和第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">11</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷中，涉及的中文名有三个：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">单叶假脈蕨属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Micromelingium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">膜蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">多脈莎草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cyperus</span></em><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">diffusus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">及其种下等级</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">宽叶多脈莎草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> C. d. var. latifolius</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">粘</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在作形容词时，“粘”读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">nian2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，正作“黏”。《植物志》中所有的“粘”字，包括属名</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">粘木属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">Ixonanthes</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（古柯科）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">粘腺果属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Commicarpus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫茉莉科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">粘冠草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Myriactis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），以及种和种下等级名如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">粘核光桃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">粘核毛桃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">粘毛香青</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">粘毛蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等，均应作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">钮</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：按《现汉》，“钮”字只有作“器物上起开关、调节等作用的部件”解和姓氏时，为正体，其他情况下为“纽”的异体字，故</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">金钮扣属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Spilanthes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">钮子瓜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Zehneria maysorensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">黄花地钮菜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Stachys xanthantha</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">柔弱黄花地钮菜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">S. x.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>gracilis</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）等名中的“钮”均应正作“纽”。纽子果</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ardisia virens</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫金牛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）的写法是正确的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">耆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：中药黄芪，《本草纲目》中作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">黄耆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，并认为“芪”是俗写。豆科黄耆属的作者即采用了这个名字。然而，事实是现在“黄芪”的使用远比“黄耆”为多，《现汉》就只收录了“黄芪”而没有收录“黄耆”。且“芪”字笔画较少，便于应用，所以《植物志》上所有的“耆”宜都改为“芪”。涉及的属名有二，即</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">黄耆属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Astragalus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">岩黄耆属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Hedysarum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（亦为豆科）；改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄芪属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">岩黄芪属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”后，还可与</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">另一个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">土黄芪属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Nogra</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">实现写法统一。此外，还有一个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">胶黄耆状棘豆</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oxytropis</span></em><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">tragacanthoides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（亦为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）宜改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">胶黄芪状棘豆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">麴</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：作“酒曲”讲时，此字是“麯”的异体字，而据《简化字总表》，麯已经简化为“曲”（但麴作姓氏时不能写作“曲”，麴曲为不同的两个姓）。虽然现在使用“麴”及其简体“麹”表示“酒曲”之义的人仍有不少，但麴字远较曲字难写，正为曲字应该是坚持贯彻的原则，故</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">鼠麴草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Gnaphalium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）应正作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鼠曲草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。其他应订正的名字还有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">鼠麴火绒草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Leontopodium forrestianum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">鼠麴蚤草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pulicaria</span></em><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">gnaphalodes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）两个。另有一个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">鼠麯雪兔子</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Saussurea gnaphalodes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（亦为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）更应简作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鼠曲雪兔子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">杓</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：杓字有二读，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> biao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时意为北斗七星的斗柄三星，此时为正体；读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">shao2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时为勺的异体。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">杓兰属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cypripedium</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兰科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）植物的唇瓣内凹呈勺形，所以这里的杓字无疑是“勺”的异体，理应正作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">勺</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。另有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">杓唇石斛</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Dendrobium moschatum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（亦为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兰科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的杓也应作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">勺</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">矢</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：上古无“屎”字，用矢假借。后来出现了“屎”字，专门表示“大便”之意，因而被文人视为俗字。一些带“屎”字的植物在文献中常被避写为“矢”，包括</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">鸡矢藤属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Paederia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">牛矢果</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">P. matsumuranus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">老鼠矢</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Symplocos stellaris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山矾科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。但在《植物志》中，带未避写的“屎”字的名字也有不少，计有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">猪屎豆属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Crotalaria</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（豆科）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">猫儿屎属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Decaisnea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木通科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸡屎树</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lasianthus hirsutus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），这些名称并没有引起使用者的不快。而且“矢”字的本义是“箭”，带矢字的植物名中，有的正是用的这个本义，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">矢车菊属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Centaurea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">矢竹属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pseudosasa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）及</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">矢叶橐吾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">矢镞叶蟹甲草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。因此，有必要恢复避写为“矢”的“屎”字，以使两字在植物中文名中的意义泾渭分明，全无混淆之虞。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(15)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蝟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蝟实属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Kolkwitzia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">忍冬科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蝟菊属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Olgaea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的蝟字，都是“猬”的异体。禾本科又有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">猬草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Hystrix</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，却不作“蝟”。一义二字，实无必要，故宜统一为“猬”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">犀：这是应用最广泛的一个异体字。包含该字的属名有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">木犀属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Osmanthus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">木犀榄属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Olea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">木犀科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">木犀草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Reseda</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">木犀草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">川犀草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oligomeris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">木犀草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">草木犀属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Melilotus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），还有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">木犀科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oleaceae </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">木犀草科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Resedaceae </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这两个科名。不难看出，种中文名“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">木犀</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Osmanthus</span></em><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">fragrans</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（通称桂花）是这些属名的基原。追本溯源的话，犀字才是正写，因为“木犀”一名由来于其木材纹理似犀角。但是后来从犀字派生出“樨”这个后起字之后，写“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">木樨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的人就越来越多，特别是在北京方言中，“木樨”已经取代“木犀”成为正体。北京的地名“木樨园”“木樨地”中的樨绝不能写作“犀”，且北京方言中“木樨”还转义指打散的鸡蛋，这里的樨字习惯也不作“犀”。普通话规范主要是以北京方言为基础的，所以《现汉》以樨字为为“木樨”一词的正体，“犀”为异体，虽然在植物学工作者看来觉得别扭，却也并非不可理解。笔者建议，宜从《现汉》，把所有犀字改为“樨”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(17)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">心</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">灯心草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Juncus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">灯心草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“心”，是“芯”的异体。虽然从字源上来看，“芯”派生自“心”（在传统的油灯的结构中，灯芯的确位于灯的中心），但现在心芯两字已经分化到了《现汉》认定“灯芯”为正体、而“灯心”为异体的程度，所以植物中文名中的这个异体宜改正过来。除该属植物外，还有灯心叶甜根子草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Saccharum spontaneum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. <em>juncifolium</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）以及科名灯心草科</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Juncaceae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中的“心”字也宜改为“芯”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">最后，《植物志》第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷上还有一个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蓧蕨属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oleandra</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其中的“蓧”是条的异体字。但在第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">6</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">分册上，修订后重新收入的此属中文名已经正作</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">条蕨属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。这个情况有必要在这里补充说明一下。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">除地名中的异体字外（为行文方便，这部分情况放到下文“别字的订正”一段中论述），仅种（含种下等级）中文名包含的异体字有（按音序排列）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">菴</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">庵</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的异体字。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">菴</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">[</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">艹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">/</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">闾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">]</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">应正作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">庵闾</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，已见上述。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">壳斗科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">菴耳柯</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lithocarpus haipinii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">也应正作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">庵耳柯</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">粃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">秕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的异体字，见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">糠粃景天</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sedum ramentaceum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">景天科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">糠粃马先蒿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis furfuracea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">迭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1964</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">年《简化字总表》旧版中规定“叠”简化为“迭”，但</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1986</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">年的新版中删掉了这一条。因此，“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">迭穗莎草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">迭叶楼梯草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">迭裂黄堇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">迭裂长蒴苣苔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">迭裂翠雀花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”（最后一个名字，《植物志》误印为“选裂翠雀花”）这几个名字中的“迭”均应作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">叠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。“迭”字用于植物名，仅见于“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">迷迭香</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">复</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：情况同上，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">1986</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">年新版《简化字总表》还规定“覆”不再简化为“复”，故“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">覆盆子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”不能再简写作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">复盆子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，所有含这一中心语的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科悬钩子属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Rubus </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">植物的中文名（如“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">覆盆子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">华北覆盆子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">拟覆盆子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”）均应正字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">稈</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">秆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的异体字。《植物志》第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷和第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">11</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷上的一些中文名，如“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">淡稈鳞盖蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">细稈湖瓜草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">节桿扁穗草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">具槽稈荸荠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”等，其中的“稈”均应正作“秆”。此外，还有一些“秆”字被误写为“桿”或“杆”，详见下文“别字的订正”一段中的分析。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">迴</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">回</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的异体字，见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">圆迴报春</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Primula ambita</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">报春花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">迴旋扁蕾</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Gentianopsis contorta</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（龙胆科）二名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">篲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">彗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的异体字，见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">篲竹</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Pseudosasa hindsii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">捲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">卷</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的异体字，见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">半扭捲马先蒿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis semitorta</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蘽</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蓬蘽</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rubus hirsutus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）一名见于《本草纲目》。其中的“蘽”字和另一个“藟”字实为一字，而后者见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葛藟葡萄</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Vitis flexuosa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葡萄科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）一名中。考虑到“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”字笔画较“蘽”为少，宜将“蘽”视为“藟”的异体字，而改蓬蘽为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓬藟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，这样可以在植物中文名中精简掉一个冷僻字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">稜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">棱</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的异体字。含有这个字的中文名如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">稜稃雀稗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">五稜藨草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">稜果海桐</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：“泡”字在《植物志》收载的中文名中，是一个意义、读音都十分复杂的字，大致有以下六种情况：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">a.</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">是㼎字的别字</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（见上文“改掉部分</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中未收录的冷僻字”一段中的论述），包括“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">小马泡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">马泡瓜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”二名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">b.</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">是藨的别字</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（见下文“别字的订正”一段中的论述），包括</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">大乌泡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">空心泡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">高粱泡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等蔷薇科悬钩子属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">Rubus </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">植物的名字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">c.</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">是脬的别字</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">马尿泡属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Przewalskia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">马尿泡</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">P. tangutica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茄科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。“尿脬”为膀胱的地方俗名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">d.</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">表示“虚而松软，不坚硬”之义</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡桐属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Paulownia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）及</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡滑竹</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Yushania mitis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡沙参</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Adenophora potaninii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桔梗科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）等。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">e.</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">表示“泡沫”“像泡沫的”之义</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pao4</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡花树属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Meliosma</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">清风藤科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）及</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡叶栒子</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡状珊瑚苣苔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡沫龙胆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡泡叶杜鹃等名</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。这些中文名里的“泡”有时是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">bullatus</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">-a</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">-um </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">之类加词的意译。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">f.</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">表示“鼓起的中空物”之义</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pao1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡果苘</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡果沙拐枣</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡囊草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等，常常是其学名中</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">-physa</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">physo-</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等词根的意译。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">可见，即便将前三种情况下的“泡”字正为其本字，“泡”字仍然有后三种意义、两种读音。最麻烦的是，其中的“泡沫”和“鼓起的中空物”两义往往不易区分，比如“泡叶”既可以理解为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">“表面呈气泡状的叶”，也可以理解为“具有鼓起中空结构的叶”，“泡果”既可以理解为“气泡状的果”，也可以理解为“鼓起而中空的果”，都符合实际，而这两义读音却是不同的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">显然，泡字的上述复杂意义和读音情况不符合植物中文名拟名应易读、易记的原则。对此，笔者从《植物志》中</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科黄芪属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">植物</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Astragalus sphaerophysa </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">被定名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">球脬黄芪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（耆）”得到启发，认为不妨把上述第六种意义的“泡”字视为“脬”的异体字。从语源上看，“脬”实际上也是从“泡”字派生而来的一个后起字，因为尿脬（膀胱）也是一种鼓起的中空物。如果把“泡果”改成“脬果”，这里的脬字可以理解为“似膀胱的”，这就既表达了“泡果”的原义，在字义上又仍可以解释得通。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这样，除了</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">马尿泡属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">之外，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡囊草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Physochlaina</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茄科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡果茜草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Microphysa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）也宜作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">脬囊草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">脬果茜草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，其他种名中的“泡果”也宜作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">脬果</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。经此处理，植物中文名中的“泡”就只剩下上述第四、第五两种含义，而这两个含义是较易区分的，这就初步解决了“泡”字释义难、读音难的问题。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">繖</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">伞</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的异体字，见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">繖花马先蒿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis umbelliformis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">繐</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">繸</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的异体字，见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">繐裂矢车菊</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Centaurea nigrescens</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">瘀</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">淤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的异体字，见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">散瘀草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ajuga pantantha</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(15)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">硃</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">朱</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的异体字，见于</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">硃毛水东哥</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Saurauia minata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">猕猴桃科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">硃砂根</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ardisia crenata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">紫金牛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）二名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">咀</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">嘴</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的俗体。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">淡黄花鸡咀咀</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oxytropis bicolor</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. <em>luteola</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">米咀闭花木</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cleistanthus pedicellatus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大戟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）应作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">淡黄花鸡嘴嘴</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”、“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">米嘴闭花木</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。惟</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">咀签属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Gouana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中的“咀”不作“嘴”，也不读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> zui3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">此外，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薰衣草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lavandula</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中的“薰”本是“熏”的异体，但熏薰二字现在的意义已经有了一定的差别。“熏”字多指令人不快的熏染，而薰字常指用香气熏染。考虑到现在“薰衣草”的写法极为流行，占绝对优势，这个属名中的异体字暂不更动。</span></p><h2 style="margin-top:8px;margin-right:14px;margin-bottom:8px;margin-left:14px;">4.<span style="font-family:宋体;">别字的订正：</span></h2><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和异体字不同，别字是指未得到语言学家认同的异写。有的别字是无心为之，有的虽然已形成一定的习惯，却是有悖于现代汉语规范的习惯，应当改正。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">《植物志》上的别字，可以再分为三种情况。一种是非地名的具有普遍性的别字，一种是地名的别字，一种是偶然出现的误写、误印。下面就分这三种情况来一一讨论（均按音序排列）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">非地名的具有普遍性的别字有（以下举属中文名以赅该属中种中文名）：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">胞</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">芽胞蹄盖蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">狭叶芽胞耳蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">芽胞叉蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”等几个蕨类名字中的“胞”，都是“</span><span
