style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">孢</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字之误。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">杈</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">杈叶槭</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Acer robustum </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">及其变种</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">河南杈叶槭</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">A. r. </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em> honanense</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">小杈叶槭</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">A. r.</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">minus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为槭树科）中的杈，都是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">叉</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”字之误。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">锤</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">棒锤瓜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Neoalsomitra</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">伏毛铁棒锤</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Aconitum flavum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛茛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“锤”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">槌</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”字之误。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">杆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字有两个读音，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gan1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时，指有一定用途的细长的木头或类似的东西，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> gan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时，指器物的像棍子的细长部分。近形字“秆”只有一个读音</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">gan3</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，指某些植物的茎。可见，这两个字意义的区别是十分清晰的，但在《植物志》上，“秆”字有时被误写为“杆”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蒿子杆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">红杆水龙骨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">直杆驼舌草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等，属名中的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">球杆毛蕨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Nesopteris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">毛杆蕨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Callistropteris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（《植物志》中本作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">球桿毛蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”、“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">毛桿蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，桿本是“杆”的异体字）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">山麻杆</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Alchornea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中的“杆”字也都是这种误写，理宜纠正。此外，有的中文名中的“杆”字用的是其本身的两个意义之一，如“花旗杆”“扁担杆”等，则不是误写，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">箭秆风</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Alpinia stachyoides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">姜科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“秆”，反倒是“杆”的误写了。还有一个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">直杆蓝桉</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eucalyptus maideni</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桃金娘科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），其中的“杆”则是“干”字之误。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">菇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">菇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”字本是真菌中的食用担子菌的通称之一，不用于被子植物。但慈姑</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sagittaria trifolia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. <em>sinensis</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（泽泻科）常常有人写成“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">慈菇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。《本草纲目》对“慈姑”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">一名的解释是：“一根岁生十二子，如慈姑之乳诸子，故以名之。”这个解释是可信的，因为慈姑的一个特征就是有球茎，且正是其食用部分，所以“慈姑”不应写用“慈菇”。《植物志》的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">慈姑属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sagittaria</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">虽然没有错，但</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">山慈菇属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Iphigenia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">百合科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">山慈菇</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Asarum sagittarioides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马兜铃科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）却错了（后者因和</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Iphigenia indica </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">重名，建议改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">岩慈姑</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，见上文第一节“改重名”中的论述）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">值得指出的是，这种在植物名字上滥加草字头的风气，正是造成许多别字的根源，下面“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">莲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">萝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">芽</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">荫</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”几个别字都属于这一情况。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">青</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">芜青</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Brassica rapa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">芜青甘蓝</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">B. napobrassica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">十字花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“青”，为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菁</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”字之误。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">勒</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">艻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：二者的同音字“簕”是粤方言，指某些具刺或刺尖的植物，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">簕竹属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bambusa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">老鼠簕属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Acanthus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">爵床科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鸡爪簕属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Oxyceros</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茜草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">簕欓花椒</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Zanthoxylum avicennae</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芸香科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）等。依此，《植物志》中的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">火殃勒</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Euphorbia antiquorum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大戟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）应为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">火殃簕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">擂鼓艻属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Mapania</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莎草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）则为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">擂鼓簕属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">之误。另外，禾本科的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">老鼠艻</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Spinifex littoreus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">也应作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">老鼠簕</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，但这就与</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">爵床科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">老鼠簕</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Acanthus ilicifolius</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">重名；事实上，这一种是其属的模式种，而属名叫“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鬣刺属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，种属名不相关，本就不合理，所以理应改名为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">鬣刺</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，既避重名，又可使种属名对应，一举两得。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">莲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">胡黄莲属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Picrorhiza</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“莲”，很显然是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">连</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的别字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">萝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字的本义是“指某些能爬蔓的植物”，所以像</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">萝藦</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Metaplexis japonica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">萝藦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">绿萝</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Epipremnum aureum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">天南星科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">茑萝松</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Quamoclit pennata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">旋花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藤萝</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Wisteria villosa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）这样的写法是正确的。但像</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">假山萝属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Harpullia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">无患子科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">山萝过路黄</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Lysimachia melampyroides</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">报春花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">山萝花马先蒿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis melampyriflora </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">假山萝花马先蒿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> P. pseudomelampyriflora</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）这样的写法则是错误的，其中的“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">萝”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字都是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">罗”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的误写（作为后三个名字的语源的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山罗花属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Melampyrum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，在《植物志》中未写错）。有的地方植物志上，还把“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">剪秋罗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">剪春罗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”等名写成“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">剪秋萝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">剪春萝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之类，一样是错误的。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">除此之外，萝字还可用于音译中。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">萝卜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Raphanus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">十字花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莳萝属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Anethum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">伞形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“萝”字是古代的音译，萝芙木属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rauvolfia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">夹竹桃科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）和葛萝槭</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Acer grosseri</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">槭树科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）是现代的音译，这些名字中的“萝”都不必纠正。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">磨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：《植物志》中，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">摩擦草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Tripsacum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">禾本科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">磨擦草属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">魔芋属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Amorphophallus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">天南星科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">磨芋属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，均误。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">稔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">菍</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：都是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">棯</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的别字。棯读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">nian1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，也是粤方言（来自古越语），指一些分布于华南地区，类似</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">桃金娘</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhodomyrtus tomentosa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（粤方言名为“岗棯”）的花瓣离生、雄蕊较多的小灌木，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄花棯属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sida</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">锦葵科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">地棯</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Melastoma dodecandrum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛棯</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">M. sanguineum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（均为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">野牡丹科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）等。在《植物志》上，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄花棯</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">棯叶扁担杆</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Grewia urenifolia </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中的棯误写为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">稔”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">地菍</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">毛菍</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">及其种下等级</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">宽萼毛菍</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Melastoma</span></em><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">sanguineum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. <em>latisepalum</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">则误写为“菍”，都应纠正。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">柠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在植物名称中，“柠”字只出现在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">柠檬</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”里。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">柠条锦鸡儿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Caragana korshinskii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“柠”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">拧</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”字之误。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：上文“异体字的订正”一段已述，在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">马泡瓜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">小马泡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”两名字，“泡”是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">㼎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的别字；在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">空心泡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">高粱泡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”等名中，“泡”是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">藨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的别字；在“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">马尿泡</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”中，“泡”是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">脬</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的别字。关于泡藨二字的关系，见下文第四节“读音的统一”中“多音字的整理”一段中的论述。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">苹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蘋</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的简化字。“蘋”有两读，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ping2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时用于“蘋果”“蘋婆”等词，《简化字总表》已规定简化为“苹”，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> pin2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时指一种蕨类植物</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Marsilea quadrifolia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蘋科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），则不能简化为“苹”，而应按“頁”的简化类推（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">GBK </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">字库中没有收这个简化字）。因此，“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蘋科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">槐叶蘋科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蘋属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">槐叶蘋属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蘋</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">埃及蘋</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">槐叶蘋</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这几个名字中的“蘋”，都不能写成“苹”。一些地方植物志（如《河北植物志》）已经注意到了这个问题，但《植物志》未能注意到，所以这几个名字在第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">6</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">分册上出现时，都写错了。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(15)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">秋</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">秋子梨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pyrus ussuriensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“秋”，是“楸”字之误。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">楸子</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Malus prunifolia </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">是同科苹果属植物，果实球形，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">楸子梨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">得名于其野生种类的果实形状、大小与楸子相似。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">苔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字有两读，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> tai1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时只用于“舌苔”一词，读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> tai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">时则指“苔藓”的“苔”。其后一读音的同音字“薹”则有三个义项，一是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，即</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Carex </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">属（莎草科）植物，二是某些植物的花莛（如“蒜薹”），三是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">芸薹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”，即</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Brassica campestris</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，为</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">十字花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">蔬菜。由于《简化字总表》规定“臺”简作“台”，有的人就把“薹”也简作“苔”，致使二字混淆，殊不知“臺”是属于不能类推的简化字，以“臺”为偏旁的字，如果《简化字总表》没有规定，其中的“臺”是绝不能简化为“台”的。《植物志》第</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">12</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">卷已经注意到了这个问题，所以“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”没有作“苔草”，但在较早出版的其他卷册中，仍有“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">泽苔草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">芸苔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">酸苔菜</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”这样的误用，均应纠正。反过来，“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">川苔草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”、“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苦苣苔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”（以及所有带“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">苣苔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的中文名）中用作拟形的“苔”字也不能写成“薹”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(17)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">葶</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字只有一个用途，即出现在复合词“葶苈”中，指十字花科的一个属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Draba</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。它有一个同音字“莛”，指的是某些植物的茎，“花莛”则指某些植物（多为无地上茎植物）的花梗或总花梗。“莛”字甚为古老，最早见于《说文解字》，至今在口语中仍有一定的使用频率（《现汉》举了一个例是“麦莛儿”），而“葶”则是很晚的后起字。因此，“莛”字在任何情况下都不应该写成“葶”，但是《植物志》恰恰相反，除了忍冬科的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">莛子藨属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Triosteum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">外，所有应该用“莛”字的地方都误用了“葶”。由此牵涉到的种级和种下等级中文名多达</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">53</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">个，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">花葶薹草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">实葶葱</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">长葶报春</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">多葶蒲公英</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">等，甚至菊科还有一个属名</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">葶菊属</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Cavea</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">也错了。这些误写的“葶”字全都应该纠正为“莛”（仅报春花科的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">葶立钟报春</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Primula firmipes</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">依其字义，正作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">亭立钟报春</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”似更好）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(18)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">芽</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：在</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">龙芽草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Agrimonia</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中，芽是“牙”的别字。这个属植物的果实顶端有钩刺，可以挂在动物的皮毛或人的衣服上传播，“龙牙”一名正是对这个特征的生动描述，写成“龙芽”则不可解。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(19)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">呆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：这个字原有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">dai1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">二读（《普通话异读词审音表》已经废除了</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的读音，统读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> dai1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）。</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">崖白菜属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Triaenophora</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）仅</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">种，分布于我国湖北省，均生于悬崖石缝中，故名。由于在湖北方言中，崖字读如普通话</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的对应音（实际上在北京土话中也有这个读音，如昌平区的地名沟崖的“崖”习惯就读</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ai2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">而不是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> ya2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">），故《植物志》玄参科作者误将此字记为“呆”，以致意义晦涩。今宜正为“崖”字，这个属名便成了一个很好地反映了生境特征的名字。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(20)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">荫</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：此字有二读，植物名字中只用</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> yin1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的读音，意为“树荫，林荫”，如</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">喜荫草属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Sciaphila</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">霉草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">林荫千里光</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Senecio nemorensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">荫生鼠尾草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Salvia umbratica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）等。但是“阴地”的阴不能写作“荫”，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">荫地冷水花</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pilea pumila</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var. <em>hamaoi</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（荨麻科）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">荫地蓼</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Polygonum umbrosum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（蓼科）中的“荫”都是“阴”的别字。此外，菊科的</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">风毛菊属</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Saussurea</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">中的“风”字，可能也是“凤”字之误。但因为风毛菊是个大属，如要改动这个字，会造成很多名字的变动，而且“风”“凤”同音不同调，改变之后会造成读音的混乱，又鉴于现在“风毛菊”这一写法远较“凤毛菊”流行，故笔者在此不做变动。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">地名的别字（为行文方便，地名中的异体字也一并放到这里讨论）有：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(1)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">巴朗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">巴朗杜鹃</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhododendron balangense</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“巴朗”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">巴郎</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。巴郎山为四川省西部邛崃山的一段。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(2)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">澂江</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：“澂”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">澄</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”的异体字，故</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">澂江狗牙花</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ervatamia chengkiangensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">夹竹桃科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）应作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">澄江狗牙花</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。澄江县位于云南省，是著名的“澄江动物群”古化石的发现地。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(3)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">葱岑</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">葱岑蒲公英</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Taraxacum pseudominutilobum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“葱岑”为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葱岭</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。葱岭为喀喇昆仑山的古称。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(4)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">丛化</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">丛化柃</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eurya metcalfiana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山茶科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“丛化”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">从化</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。从化为广东省市名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(5)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">大砲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：“砲”是“炮”的异体字，故大砲马先蒿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis tapaoensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）应作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">大炮马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。大炮山为邛崃山山峰名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(6)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">峨嵋</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：峨眉山，旧亦作“峨嵋山”，现在的地名标准化规范中已将“嵋”字作为异体。故此，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">峨嵋溲疏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Deutzia pilosa</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（虎耳草科）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">峨嵋马先蒿</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Pedicularis omiiana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）应正作“峨眉溲疏”和“峨眉马先蒿”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(7)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">鸳銮鼻</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">鸳銮鼻铁线莲</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Clematis terniflora </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em>garanbiensis</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛茛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“鸳銮鼻”是“鹅銮鼻”之误。鹅銮鼻为台湾岛的最南端。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(8)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">风庆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">风庆小檗</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Berberis holocraspedon</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">小檗科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">风庆豆腐柴</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Premna crassa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>yui</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">马鞭草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“风庆”均是“凤庆”之误。凤庆为云南县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(9)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蒿苹</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">蒿苹四蕊槭</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Acer tetramerum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>haopingense</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">槭树科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“蒿苹”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蒿坪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。蒿坪为陕西省太白山小地名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(10)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">井岗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">井岗柳</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Salix leveilleana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杨柳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">井岗山杜鹃</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Rhododendron jinggangshanicum</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杜鹃花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“井岗”均是“井冈”之误。井冈山位于江西省井冈山市境内，是著名的革命老区。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(11)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">禄春</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">禄春谷木</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Memecylon luchuenense</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">野牡丹科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">禄春安息香</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Styrax macranthus</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">安息香科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“禄春”均是“绿春”之误。绿春为云南省红河哈尼族彝族自治州县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(12)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">木坪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">木坪金粉蕨</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Onychium moupinense</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">中国蕨科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“木坪”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">穆坪</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。穆坪镇是四川省宝兴县政府驻地。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(13)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">纳拥</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">纳拥合耳菊</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> Synotis nayongensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“纳拥”为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">纳雍</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。纳雍为贵州西部县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(14)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">南头</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">南头大头茶</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Gordonia axillaris var. nantoensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">山茶科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“南头”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">南投</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。南投为台湾县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(15)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">普蓝</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">普蓝翠雀花</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Delphinium pulanense</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛茛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“普蓝”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">普兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。普兰为西藏县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(16)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">清河</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">清河糙苏</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Phlomis chinghoensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“清河”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">青河</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。青河为新疆县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(17)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">邱北</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">邱北冬蕙兰</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cymbidium qiubeiense</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兰科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">邱北铁线莲</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Clematis chiupehensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">毛茛科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">邱北猪屎豆</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Crotalaria qiubenensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">豆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“邱北”都是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">丘北</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。丘北县为云南省红河哈尼族彝族自治州县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(18)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">搭山</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">搭山獐牙菜</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Swertia tozanensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">龙胆科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“搭山”为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">塔山</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。塔山为台湾阿里山脉的主峰。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(19)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">大鲁阁</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">大鲁阁叉柱兰</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Cheirostylis tatawakii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">兰科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">大鲁阁小米草</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Euphrasia tarokoana</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">玄参科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“大鲁阁”均是“太鲁阁”之误。太鲁阁为台湾地名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(20)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">太山</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">太山柳</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Salix taishanensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杨柳科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“太山”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">泰山</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。泰山位于山东省泰安市境内，为五岳之一，是中华名山。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(21)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">武葳山</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">台湾枇杷武葳山变型</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Eriobotrya deflexa</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> f.<em> buisanensis</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蔷薇科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“武葳山”是“武藏山”之误。武藏山为台湾东部山峰名。按上文第二节“和种下等级有关的中文名订正”中论述的种下等级命名订正法，这个名字应正作“武藏山枇杷”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(22)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">西周</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">西周赤瓟</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Thladiantha nudiflora </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em>bracteata</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">葫芦科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“西周”为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">西固</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。西固现为甘肃省兰州市市辖区名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(23)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">雅龙江</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">雅龙江风毛菊</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Saussurea hultenii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“雅龙江”为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">雅砻江</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。雅砻江是长江支流，四川西部著名大河。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(24)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">英吉利</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">英吉利茶藨子</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ribes palczewskii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">虎耳草科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“英吉利”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">英吉里</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">之误。英吉利是</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">English</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（意译为“英格兰的”）的音译，英吉里是大兴安岭山峰名，可谓差之毫厘，谬以千里。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(25)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">越隽</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">越隽川木香</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Dolomiaea denticulata</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">菊科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“越隽”为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">越嶲</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。越嶲为四川省西南部县名（今作越西）。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(26)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">扎多</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">扎多点地梅</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Androsace alaschanica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>zadoensis</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">报春花科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“扎多”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">杂多</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。杂多为青海县名。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">(27)</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">准喀尔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">：</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">准喀尔黄芩</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Scutellaria soongorica</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">唇形科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“准喀尔”是“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">准噶尔</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”之误。准噶尔为来自蒙古语的地域名，指我国新疆北部准噶尔盆地一带。另外，</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">阿墩小檗</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Berberis muliensis </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var.<em> atuntzeana</em></span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（小檗科）和</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">阿墩紫堇</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Corydalis atuntsuensis</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">（</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">罂粟科</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">）中的“阿墩”，为阿墩子的简称。阿墩子是云南省德钦县政府驻地升平镇的旧称，为藏语音译，简为“阿墩”是不恰当的，上述二类群的加词也是“阿墩子”全名的拉丁文对写，并未省去“子”字。何况《植物志》中另有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阿墩子龙胆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阿墩子马先蒿</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阿墩子假冷蕨</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阿墩子虎耳草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">四名，其中的“阿墩子”并未简称。为统一、准确起见，“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">阿墩小檗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">阿墩紫堇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”应正作“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阿墩子小檗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”和“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">阿墩子紫堇</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">需要说明的是，上述订正仅限于地名中的异体字、别字；由于政区的变革造成的地名改变则未予考虑。如海南省崖县，今为三亚市，但“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">崖县扁担杆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">崖县球兰</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">崖县叶下珠</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”并不改名为“三亚扁担杆”“三亚球兰”“三亚叶下珠”。这是因为政区的变动是年年都在发生的，如果要求植物名称中的政区名也随之变动，不仅有违保持植物中文名稳定的原则，而且改不胜改。同理，虽然四川省越嶲县今已简写成越西县，但上面提到的越嶲川木香也不作“越西川木香”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">此外，禾本科还有一个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">波陂雀麦</span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Bromus popovii</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">，其中的“波陂”是种加词</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> popovii </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">的音译，而这个种加词来源于俄罗斯姓氏</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Popov</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">。虽然音译比较自由，用“波陂”来译</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">popovii </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">本身并无不妥，但“陂”不仅是个冷僻字，还是个多音字，有</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> bei1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">po1</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">、</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">pi2</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">三读，在《植物志》植物名称中，“陂”字仅此一用，仅为了这一个音译就使用一个冷僻字、多音字，是有违植物中文拟名易记、易读的原则的，故笔者建议这种植物的中文名按</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"> Popov </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">这个姓氏的通译“波波夫”，改为“</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">波波雀麦</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">”。</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">最后，属于偶然出现的误写、误印，有下面这些名字（按原名音序排列），就不一一解释了：</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">误</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">正</span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">学名</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;"></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">长果锣锅底</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;"><br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">长果罗锅底</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"><br  /></span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Hemsleya macrosperma</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em>oblongcarpa</em></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">长叶钮子果</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;"><br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">长叶纽子果</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Ardisia virens</span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"> var.<em> annamensis</em></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">称杆树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;"><br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">秤杆树</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"><br  /></span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Maesa ramentacea</span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">二岐山蚂蝗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;"><br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">二歧山蚂蝗</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"><br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Desmodium dichotomum</span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">甘菊稳舌甘菊变种</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">隐舌甘菊</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"><br  /></span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Dendranthema lavandulifolium </span></em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">var. <em>discoideum</em></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">观尝龙胆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;"><br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">观赏龙胆</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"><br  /></span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Gentiana prolata</span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">黄岑母草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;"><br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">黄芩母草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#5B9BD5;"> </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;"></span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Lindernia scutellariiformis</span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">及已</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;"><br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">及己</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <br  /></span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Chloranthus serratus</span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">结壮飘拂草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;"><br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">结状飘拂草</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;"><br  /></span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Fimbristylis rigidula</span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">兰猪耳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;"><br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#5B9BD5;">蓝猪耳</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <br  /></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><em><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#47C1A8;">Torenia fournieri</span></em></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">骆驼逢</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;color:#FFA000;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <em>mongolica</em></span></p><p style="text-indent:24px;"><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;">还有一个</span><span style="font-size:12px;font-family:宋体;color:#FFA000;">矽镁马先蒿</span><em><span
